            var t = document.createElement("script"), n = document.createAttribute("type");
            n.value = "text/javascript", t.attributes.setNamedItem(n), d = document.createAttribute("defer"), d.value = "defer", t.attributes.setNamedItem(d);
            var o = document.createAttribute("src");
            o.value = e, t.attributes.setNamedItem(o), document.body.appendChild(t)
        }), document.bindReady(function () {
            document.appendHeadStyle();
            for (var e = 0; e < window.iasonScripts.length; e++) document.appendBodyScript(window.iasonScripts[e])
        });
        var iasonLoadEndOfBody = !0;
    }
       </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   /* <![CDATA[ */
    function nscout() {
      if (document.all) {
        allLinks = document.all.tags("A");
      } else if (document.documentElement) {
        allLinks = document.getElementsByTagName("A");
      }
      if (typeof(allLinks) != "undefined") {
        for (i = 0; i < allLinks.length; i++) {
          if (allLinks[i].getAttribute('class') && allLinks[i].getAttribute('class').match(new RegExp("(^|\\s)nscout(\\s|$)"))) {
            if (allLinks[i].href.indexOf('hamburg.de/') == -1) {
              allLinks[i].setAttribute('data-extern-link-target', allLinks[i].href);
            }
          }
          if (allLinks[i].getAttribute('class') && allLinks[i].getAttribute('class').match(new RegExp("(^|\\s)nscout pdf(\\s|$)"))) {
            allLinks[i].setAttribute('data-download_pdf-link-target', allLinks[i].href);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    nscout();
    /* ]]> */
  </script>
